The Dissolution of the Ninth Army Corps 88

The armies in North China previously had army corps organizations during the Anti-Japanese War. Now that the situation is peaceful, the organization of the armies urgently needs to be reduced. Song Zheyuan's Second Army Corps has been ordered to dissolve a few days ago. Song will continue to serve as the commander of the 29th Army. The Ninth Army Corps, Sun Dianying's unit, also received an order from the Military Branch Committee today (14th) to dissolve the army corps organization. After receiving the order, Sun has issued a notice to his subordinates to immediately abolish the name of the Ninth Army Corps. Sun will continue to serve as the commander of the 41st Army. As for Sun's unit's westward departure from Baotou to reclaim land in Qinghai, it is currently being actively prepared. Sun has ordered his engineering corps and supply teams to depart from Baotou and head towards Wuyuan and Ninghe, rushing to dig wells, repair roads, set up tents, purchase supplies, etc. The forward stations of each brigade also departed from Baotou one after another on the 12th. All troops will begin their westward movement from Baotou after the forward stations arrive in Wuyuan. (14th)

Feng Yuxiang's Thoughts on the September 18th Incident 89

How to Commemorate September 18th?

Anti-Japanese Resistance Should Focus on Implementation

Jinan Correspondence: After concluding his affairs in Chahar, Feng Yuxiang returned to Tai'an and has not changed his original intention of resisting Japan and saving the country. As the second anniversary of the painful September 18th Incident approaches, Feng has specially published "How to Commemorate September 18th?" The text is recorded as follows:

It has been two years since the September 18th Incident. Although the capital has been moved back to Nanjing and the salaries of government personnel have been restored to their original levels, a superficial appearance of peace and prosperity seems to have returned. However, the lost territory of the three northeastern provinces has not been recovered. On the contrary, Rehe and Yu Guan have been lost. After the Tanggu Truce was established, Luandong was nominally received, but the Japanese intervened in bandit suppression. The Japanese do not allow intervention in Xinglong County's territory outside the Great Wall. They openly stated that the Great Wall line is the border of Manchuria. These are obvious facts that have been published in various newspapers. These facts clearly prove that the current difficulties are deeper than they were a year ago. The deeper the difficulties, the more silent the reaction. Slogans such as resisting goods, preparing for war, and resisting Japan have gradually vanished like smoke. This is truly a major crisis for our country. Before the lost territory is recovered, all of our citizens should bear the responsibility of resisting Japan. Those who bear heavy responsibilities for national affairs need not be said. Regardless of the method of resisting Japan, whether it is long-term resistance or (resistance while negotiating), the word "resistance" must not be abandoned. More importantly, "resistance" must be put into practice. There must be facts in front of the compatriots. Otherwise, it will inevitably form a verbal mantra of "resistance", only deceiving oneself and others. I have always advocated resisting Japan, especially advocating armed resistance. Therefore, I must practice what I preach. At the time of the crisis in Peiping and Tianjin, I was deceived by the patriotic sentiment for Rehe, ignoring my strength and avoiding danger, collecting volunteers to fight the Japanese puppets, hoping to preserve Chahar and recover the lost territory as an example to the world. After several bloody battles, more than 1,600 brave soldiers were killed or wounded. Fortunately, Shichang, Kangbao, Guyuan, Duolun, and other places were successively recovered, which caused the Japanese puppets and traitors to falsely accuse me of communism and separatism, attempting to disrupt international public opinion and incite internal disputes in our country. I only want to resist Japan, and of course, I strive for peace internally. I also received notification from the government officials, Wang Jingwei and Chiang Kai-shek, that the central government has a whole plan for resisting Japan. Since there is a whole plan for resisting Japan, even though we do not know its content, in order to avoid internal disputes, we have to retreat and listen to the government to implement its whole plan. Therefore, on August 6th, all military and political powers were completely handed over to the government. However, in this practical anti-Japanese struggle, I have gained several understandings: (1) The people and soldiers are indeed determined to resist Japan. In the serious period of national crisis, the anti-Japanese atmosphere has been silent. Therefore, it is generally believed that the people and soldiers are not supportive. In fact, this is not the case. The people and soldiers are indeed patriots. During this recovery of eastern Chahar, in the deserted areas where there was no food or lodging, the Anti-Japanese Allied Army was welcomed and helped by the people everywhere and acted as guides for our army. They all scrambled to disrupt the rear of the Japanese puppet army. The Allied Army was temporarily formed by various scattered anti-Japanese troops. They lacked food and clothing, and were short of ammunition. They were in the rain, walking in the wilderness. However, as soon as they heard the order to attack, they all bravely sacrificed themselves. It can be seen that the military and popular sentiments are full of anti-Japanese enthusiasm. The reason why the anti-Japanese atmosphere is depressed is just that they have not been given the opportunity to express it. (2) The Anti-Japanese War must have a plan and unified command. In the Battle of the Great Wall, our hundreds of thousands of troops were not unfaithful or brave, but the failure was due to the lack of a unified plan and command. This may be a major reason. This time, the recovery of eastern Chahar was far less than the strength of the Battle of the Great Wall. Moreover, it was also a joint army, not an entire system of troops. However, the reason why it was effective was that it was more planned and the command was unified. Therefore, after I sent a telegram on the same day to hand over all political power, the Military Branch Committee announced that Duolun had been lost again on the 13th. It is thought that the lack of unified command in the transition of military and political power was also an important cause of the failure. Based on the above observations, although the anti-Japanese atmosphere is depressed, the patriotic heart of the people is not indifferent. Although the Anti-Japanese War has failed, it is not entirely impossible to fight. The government has repeatedly said that it has a plan for resisting Japan, which is what all our compatriots are praying for. It seems that in the crisis of national crisis, there is no way to save oneself. The important thing is to implement it.

Therefore, our current commemoration of September 18th is not about verbal disputes. It should be to resist Japan, which is already well known to the people. In the future, we should all determine the method of resisting Japan and practice it personally. Even if there are some concerns and obstacles, as long as we can persevere to the end and do our part to resist Japan, we will naturally have results. Otherwise, the facts are obvious, and even if we are good at defending ourselves, we cannot cover up our mistakes. In the past, I have repeatedly made suggestions to the government regarding the plan for resisting Japan. People from all walks of life have also made many famous comments. However, now that more territory has been lost and the country is weaker, and the commemoration of September 18th has reached two years, I believe that the current commemoration of September 18th is about (implementing anti-Japanese resistance). All the things I have said before, such as consolidating national defense, recovering lost territory, and resisting goods, will not be repeated. However, in the course of implementing anti-Japanese resistance, military preparedness must be emphasized, and political aspects must also be reformed. In terms of the people, they should have a spirit of fearlessness, unite with each other, supervise the government, and eliminate traitors to achieve the anti-Japanese spirit. In terms of the government, it should allow the people to express their anti-Japanese opinions as much as possible and develop anti-Japanese forces as much as possible. Foreign affairs and finance must be completely open, so that suspicions can be dispelled and the support of the people can be obtained. In terms of the national economy, efforts should be made to revive it, and the boundless economic aggression of imperialism should not be allowed, or even to promote the sale of surplus products for it. In terms of politics, efforts should be made to eliminate corruption and rectify discipline. These are the minimum reforms that must be made at present. If not, the country will not be a country, how can we talk about resistance? Even if there is the largest meeting and the most eloquent speech, it will not be enough to commemorate September 18th, and the shame of September 18th will increase year by year until it is dragged into the Second World War and perish with the country. Even if we make statements that fill the court, what benefit will it bring to the country? Therefore, the commemoration of September 18th must be in (implementing anti-Japanese resistance).

Economic Committee Dredges the Huayang River 90

Has Ordered the Jiangxi-Jiangxi Engineering Bureau to Send Personnel for Surveying

Giant Sluice Gate to be Built at the River Mouth to Control Tides and Water Flow

Wuhu Correspondence: The Huayang River is located at the junction of the three provinces of Anhui, Hubei, and Jiangxi. It originates from the Huangpeng Lake and extends to the mouth of the Yangtze River, stretching for more than 400 li. Recently, it has not been dredged for many years, the riverbed is silted up, and the inland lakes are wide and unfathomable. Every time the tide comes, the river flows back, and the river channel often suffers from blockage, resulting in the flooding of about 40 million mu of polder fields along the river, which cannot be saved. The benefits are abandoned on the land, which is very regrettable. Recently, the National Economic Commission has accepted the request of the people from the seven counties connected to the rivers in the three provinces and decided to start dredging immediately. Because the river connects large lakes internally and large rivers externally, the water势悬殊, and it will not be effective without control in the event of a tide, it was decided to build a giant sluice gate at the river mouth. The Wuhu-Jiangxi Engineering Bureau has been ordered to send personnel for surveying in order to plan construction. After receiving the order, the bureau immediately sent three surveying teams to work, with two teams surveying the water flow and one team surveying the water surface. It is estimated that after the Huayang River is dredged and the sluice gate is built, the water flow can be controlled on time, and at the very least, 10 million mu of arable land can be obtained for migration and cultivation, which will benefit the country and the people, which is no small matter.

Wang Baozhai, the Administrative Inspector Commissioner of the Second District of Anhui Province and the Magistrate of Wuhu County, believes that most of the areas under his jurisdiction are riverside areas in southern Anhui. When the Yangtze River flooded during the 20th year of the Republic of China, he still thought that the unexpected event was accidental. Since then, however, dangerous situations have often occurred every time the flood season arrives, and special situations have become constant. The fertile areas will be flooded. Recently, he has specially drafted a (Letter of Opinions on Preventing Floods in the Middle and Lower Reaches of the Yangtze River) and submitted it to the Anhui Provincial Government, the Department of Construction, and the Headquarters, requesting adoption. The content is divided into (A) Causes of Floods in the Middle and Lower Reaches of the Yangtze River: 1. The river channel is becoming narrower, which is not enough to provide for the discharge of floods; 2. Reclaiming abandoned lakes into fields makes it difficult to slow down the rapid water flow; 3. Siltation has accumulated for many years, and the riverbed has become shallower; 4. The embankments are exposed to waves and lose their protection. (B) Fundamental Measures to Control Floods: 1. It is forbidden to reclaim wasteland and abandoned lakes in the future; 2. Reeds and willows should be planted on the river beaches near the dikes; 3. The riverbed should be dredged to make the depth reasonable. (13th)

Southern Route Army Bombs Junmen Ridge 91

The Jiangxi Bandits Have a Tendency to Withdraw from Huichang

Nanchang Correspondence: After the Red bandits Zhu De and Mao Zedong suffered losses in the Yihuang campaign in June, they again practiced feigning a move to the east while attacking in the west, using only a small number of scattered bandits and a portion of ragtag bandits to advance towards Yongfeng and Jishui east of the central section of the Gan River, pretending to cross the Gan River westward. In fact, they moved all their main forces eastward, marching at night and hiding during the day, to attack western Fujian. Fang Shao and other bandits from Lichuan and Zixi were divided by Chongcheng, Guangze, and Shaowu, secretly attacking northern Fujian and echoing each other. In terms of southern Jiangxi, they adopted a defensive battle to prevent the Southern Route Army from cutting off their retreat. In terms of eastern Jiangxi, they adopted a contraction policy, using a small number of bandits to carry out guerrilla warfare in dangerous mountainous areas to contain the government forces. This is the general outline of the Red bandits' movements in the past two months of July and August. Therefore, since June, military affairs in northwestern Fujian have become increasingly tense, and there have been fierce battles in Liancheng and Yanping. There have also been frequent contacts between Huichang and Anyuan on the Jiangxi-Guangdong border. However, the northern and western routes of Jiangxi Province have been relatively quiet, so the armies on these two routes have focused all their efforts on reorganizing and replenishing their forces, improving themselves, and preparing for combat. At present, the bandit suppression armies on all routes are about to take unified action to launch a general offensive against the bandits. According to public announcements, the Guangdong Army has launched a large-scale bombing of the Red bandit fortifications on Junmen Ridge, which has been very successful. The Red bandits there have a tendency to withdraw from Huichang. Junmen Ridge is located south of Huichang, east to Wuping and Shanghang in Fujian, south to Pingyuan and Meixian in Guangdong, and west to Anyuan and Xunwu. It is a transportation hub for the three provinces. In the past, it was an important tax checkpoint in Jiangxi. The mountains are dense and it is easy to defend and difficult to attack. Therefore, the Red bandits focused on guarding it, on the one hand to cover the attack on Fujian, and on the other hand to consolidate the Ruijin base area where the puppet central government is located. The Guangdong Army, in order to aid Fujian, previously attacked Junmen Ridge from Xunwu and Anyuan. However, the bandits were familiar with the terrain and the fortifications were solid, so the Southern Route Army has made no special progress. Now that the Southern Route Army has deployed a large number of aircraft, they are flying to bomb it every day. It is reported that the bandit's blockhouses, gun emplacements, earthen forts, and all fortifications near Chengjiang, Qingxi, Wantiankeng, and Junmen Ridge have been destroyed. In general, the Southern Route Army can advance on a large scale, and the Red bandits there have a tendency to withdraw from Huichang. If the Southern Route Army occupies Huichang, then taking Ruijin will be like taking something out of a bag. (September 13th)

Deng Shizeng Arrives in Guangdong 92

Commissioned by Jiang Guangnai and Cai Tingkai

To Discuss Cooperation with Chen Jitang in Suppressing Bandits

Guangzhou Correspondence: Since the Jiangxi bandits turned to attack Yanping in western Fujian, the situation in Fujian has become tense. The 19th Route Army has specially sent Deng Shizeng, the chief of staff of the Fuzhou Pacification Commissioner's Office, to Guangdong to discuss important issues such as coordinating with Guangdong in suppressing bandits and requesting Guangdong authorities to assist with military expenses. Deng arrived in the province on the morning of the 9th and immediately went to Meihua Village in Dongshan to visit Chen Jitang and convey the personal letters from Jiang Guangnai and Cai Tingkai to Chen. It is reported that the Fujian authorities' opinions, in addition to discussing the political issues of the current situation, also hope that Guangdong can dispatch troops to enter western Fujian from Shanghang as soon as possible to attack Changting in a pincer movement to contain the bandits in northern Fujian, and to attack Junmen as soon as possible to destroy the bandit nests in eastern Jiangxi. In addition, the Fujian authorities sent a telegram to Guangdong a few days ago, stating that Guangdong Province is assisting the 19th Route Army with 200,000 yuan per month for military expenses. Now, due to the urgency of military affairs, Deng has also requested Guangdong to remit the assistance for September in advance and to borrow 200,000 rounds of water-cooled machine gun bullets and various rifle bullets. Chen Jitang has agreed to handle the assistance as requested, but the borrowing of bullets needs to be investigated for storage numbers before a decision can be made. According to Deng, his mission here is to discuss various bandit suppression plans with Chen Jitang. Once the discussion is settled, he will return to Fujian immediately. As for the rumors that Yanping has fallen, it is inaccurate. However, it is true that Yanping is trapped by bandits. There are only about 20,000 bandits, most of whom are vagrants. The bandits dare not attack our fortified positions. They only covet and harass places with weak forces. The number of provincial defense troops in northern Fujian is limited, so recently the bandit forces have moved from west to north. Now Commander-in-Chief Cai has transferred Mao Weishou and Tan Qixiu to suppress the bandit atmosphere. There will be no major problems in northern Fujian. However, it will take time to clear out these fleeing bandits. It is said that Deng will stay in Guangdong for a few days before returning to Fujian to report. (September 10th)

Drowned Body Found in Xiaomeng Jiang Temple, Songjiang 93

An unidentified male body was found in the river next to the railway in Xiaomeng Jiang Temple, 15th District. He was about 30 years old, wearing a blue cloth short shirt and pants, and Zhongshan shoes with no socks. There was a stone wound on the right corner of his head, and his skull was broken. He was lying face down, with mud on his back. The villagers observed that he seemed to have fallen from the train. The township police reported the case to the procuratorate for inspection. Today, the prosecutor led officials to the village by car to verify the facts, filled out the corpse form, and waited for a notice to be issued for collection.

County Government Meeting Discusses Converting Farmland to Grain Delivery 94

Our county's areas of Punan, Shanyang, Caojing, Zhalin, and other places are located near the coast, and the soil is poor, which is different from Pubei. Therefore, it has always been farmland converted to grain delivery. Since the 18th year, the provincial authorities ordered the conversion to grain delivery. Farmers in Fengxian and Jinshan counties also requested the provincial authorities to withdraw their orders. After dispatching commissioners to conduct on-site surveys, it was found that Fengxian and Jinshan counties were temporarily allowed to postpone the conversion. However, Songjiang County was uniquely different. The local tenants heard about this and ran around telling each other. They jointly presented appeals to the provincial authorities, but the accumulated cases have not been resolved to this day. This time, the Department of Finance sent commissioners to urge the collection of taxes. County Magistrate Jin took the opportunity to convene farmers from various warehouses in Punan to discuss solutions. It has now been resolved that, starting this year, 40% of the original increased tax amount will be collected. As for the taxes owed after the 18th year, they will be discussed with the farmers when they return to their hometowns, and a report will be submitted to the county and then to the province for remission in order to alleviate the people's difficulties.

Wuxi Jail Warden Han Transferred to Zhenjiang 95

The warden of the county jail in our county, Han Yuwen, recently found that the old prison buildings were dilapidated and the prisoners were crowded. It was urgent to add new prisons, so he drafted a plan and submitted it to the county government for approval. County Magistrate Yan ordered the director of the technical office, Zhang Fulin, to send technician Shen Caiyi to investigate. They are now actively drawing plans and designs, preparing to build more than 40 new prison rooms. The construction cost is 60,000 yuan. The High Court has agreed to allocate 10,000 yuan. Lu Bohong, a philanthropist in Shanghai, has also generously agreed to donate 14,000 yuan. Warden Han also plans to auction off the base and buildings of the prison branch office west of the county government, which is estimated to be worth 10,000 yuan. The rest will be raised locally, and there is considerable certainty. Yesterday, the county government suddenly received an order from the High Court to transfer Warden Han to Zhenjiang, and Kong Xianglin was appointed to fill the vacancy in Wuxi. The new and old wardens are required to take over on October 1st. After receiving the order, County Magistrate Yan has already transferred the order to Warden Han to handle the closing affairs. The matter of adding new prisons will still proceed as usual. It is heard that the High Court transferred Han to Zhenjiang this time because Zhenjiang is also adding new prisons, and all the plans are entrusted to Han to handle.

Rice Industry Deduction Dispute Reconciled Again 96

The local rice and bean industry has always had a 99 deduction for consignment sales, that is, one fen is deducted for every yuan. This year, the trade association decided to change the 99 deduction to 98.4, but the rice merchants in the Beiting section expressed opposition and were in a confrontation with the Sanliqiao section. Although various parties have been running around to mediate, the stalemate has not been resolved due to the extreme positions of both sides. Zhao Zixin, the chairman of the Rice Industry Association, seeing the situation, believed that the long-term unresolved dispute would be extremely detrimental to the reputation of the industry. Therefore, he specially sent someone to Suzhou to invite Zhou Hongqing, a standing committee member of the Suzhou Chamber of Commerce and a rice industry tycoon, to Wuxi for mediation. Zhou arrived in Wuxi yesterday and is staying in Room 26 of the Railway Hotel. He has contacted Chen Zilin, the leader of the rice industry in the Beiting section of our county, once and has scheduled to convene both parties at the Miscellaneous Grain Association today to carry out mediation work and jointly seek solutions.

Nanhui Pirates Rob Official Salt Ship, Resist Arrest and Fight 97

At Donghai Beach in Laogang Town, this county, a large motorized sailboat suddenly arrived the day before yesterday. It was said to be from Yuyao, fully loaded with over one thousand five hundred packages of official salt, intending to sail to Liuhe. Unexpectedly, when it sailed across the Nicheng waters of this county, five pirates, all armed with box guns, swarmed onto the ship, confining the eleven boatmen in the front cabin. The pirates then steered the ship to a mooring point. The pirates went ashore and declared that they had several packages of private salt and were willing to sell them at reduced prices. At that time, Zhu Dongkui's wife from the town, and the female owner of the Nanshan Hall pharmacy, nicknamed Little White, were willing to promote the sale. Just as they were unloading the salt packages, they were discovered by the anti-smuggling patrol team stationed at Huangjia Road, who immediately dispatched police to arrest them. They also rushed to report to the tax police branch in this city, and telegraphed the Lujiahui and Datuan branches to assist in the arrest. When the tax police from each team arrived at the town, the pirates, seeing the situation was unfavorable, took the initiative and opened fire. The tax police immediately returned fire, and after a fierce battle for about half an hour, the pirates were unable to hold out and jumped into the water to escape. Zhu Dongkui's wife was shot and wounded on the spot. The ship was seized by the police and escorted to Liuhe.

Robbery Occurs in Jiashan Suburb 98

The home of Yao Jinfu, a resident of Xubang Village in the eastern suburbs of this county, was suddenly broken into by more than ten robbers last night. They ransacked the house, stealing a large quantity of white rice and silver dollars. Before leaving, they also stole a civilian boat. By the time the city's security corps and public security bureau received the news and went to arrest them, the bandits had already fled far away.

Major Theft Case in Zhonghe Alley, City 99

The home of wealthy gentleman Qian Wanyi in Zhonghe Alley in this county was burgled last night (the night of the 14th). Thieves stole approximately two thousand yuan worth of silver dollars, jewelry, and gold bracelets, not to mention the soft goods and valuable fur clothing. By the time the victim discovered the theft, the thieves had already escaped. He reported the incident to the public security bureau, who conducted an investigation and strictly ordered the land and water police teams to investigate and arrest the perpetrators at all transportation points. Qian Wanyi, who works in the provincial party headquarters, rushed back to his hometown overnight upon hearing the news to investigate the case.

Collapse of the Baimao Tang Dike in Changshu 100

The Baimao Tang dike suffered from severe erosion due to the hurricane and strong tidal surge that passed through the area the day before yesterday. Over the past few days, more than two hundred zhang [~667 meters] of the dike have gradually collapsed. If the water level rises again, the farmland on both sides of the dike will inevitably be flooded, which is a matter of great concern. The district office has reported to the county government and requested an appropriation to repair the dike to protect the farmland.

Breach of the Sanyu Seawall in Nantong Causes Disaster 101

The Sanyu seawall in Nantong was breached by tidal surges, causing severe flooding and a disastrous situation. Chen Yizhong, the director of the public security bureau, surveyed the disaster situation on the 14th and reported to the county government, stating that seawater had overflowed the dikes and multiple breaches had occurred. At one point, floodwaters raged, turning the Dongyu, Jinnan, and Dadong districts into a swamp. The nearly ripe cotton and bean crops in the disaster area were submerged by the tidal surge. Many houses were also destroyed. Countless children drowned, and pigs, sheep, chickens, and dogs were almost entirely wiped out. The victims, supporting the elderly and carrying the young, were left homeless, crying by the roadside, begging for food, their plight too miserable to describe. Fortunately, the tidal surge has now gradually receded. Workers are being supervised to rush to repair the breaches and provide post-disaster relief.

Adulterous Woman Fails to Murder Husband 102

Zhang Gui, an adulterous woman from Xiting, colluded with her lover Ji Yongquan to murder her husband, Zhang Bao. Their plan was seen by his twelve-year-old daughter, Lin Xiu, who cried for help. The adulterer and adulteress fled. They have now been apprehended by the public security bureau and handed over to the court for trial.

Ministry of Railways Convenes Unified Accounting Committee in Nanjing 103

Since Zhang Jingli was appointed as the accounting director of the Ministry of Railways by the National Government's Directorate-General of Budget, Accounting and Statistics, Mr. Zhang has been acting on the orders of the Minister of Railways and the Director-General of Budget, Accounting and Statistics, vigorously rectifying the accounting department. The selection of heads of accounting offices has been based on expertise and experience in railway accounting. Therefore, significant results have been achieved in the past two years. Now, to further improve and unify the accounting and statistics of various railways, a general meeting is scheduled to be convened on the 19th of this month. At that time, the heads of the accounting offices of various railways, the chief auditors, and the responsible section chiefs of the accounting office of the Ministry of Railways will be required to attend and discuss matters of mutual concern. It is also reported that Zhang Yuhua, the head of the general affairs of the meeting, along with Secretary Ou Fusong, clerk Wu Yinghao, and others, have prepared everything for the meeting.

Zhenjiang Requests Exemption from Fishing Tax for Shengshan 104

Chongming Shengshan is an isolated island surrounded by water. The nearby residents all make a living by fishing. Last week's hurricane and torrential rain caused a disaster, with fishermen injured or killed and no fewer than a thousand fishing boats capsized. It was a rare catastrophe in recent years. The county government, in view of the fishermen's suffering, has specially requested the Department of Construction to provide relief to comfort the victims. After receiving the report, the Department of Construction, in addition to ordering the Chongming County Government to provide relief, has forwarded a request to the Ministry of Industry to instruct the Chongming Fisheries Improvement Association's collection office to immediately exempt Shengshan from fishing taxes.

The Jiangsu Military Law Trial Office is Abolished 105

The Jiangsu Provisional Military Law Trial Office has recently received an order from the provincial government, which in turn received a clear order from the National Government, to abolish it. After receiving the order, Director Qian Jiaxiang ordered the office to expedite the closing procedures. It is reported that the office's current prisoners, who have been handed over by various counties, will, except for important criminals who will be handed over to the Security Office, be sent back to their original counties to be dealt with according to law. Yesterday, Director Qian specially instructed Shen, the battalion commander of the Security Office's Special Service Battalion, to send a team to escort the criminals back to their original counties. After receiving the instruction, Battalion Commander Shen ordered his subordinates yesterday to send teams to escort them to Taixing, Gaoyou, Taizhou, and other counties separately. It is reported that there are more than seventy criminals in total.

Inspectors in Huzhou Paraded Through the Streets as a Warning 106

The Yongfengrun Cloth Store in this city recently had eight boxes of factory cloth shipped from Shanghai via Lixing. On the afternoon of the twelfth, coolies were hired to transport them. While passing the Kaitai Mat Store entrance at the Zidiling intersection on North Street, they were stopped by anti-Japanese association inspectors Zhu Baoshun, Zhu Baoxing, Cai Zhaogen, and others, who ordered the coolies to stop, intending to open the boxes for inspection. The coolies said that if they wanted to inspect, they should open them inside the store, as it was not convenient on the road. While they were arguing, a clerk from the Kaitai Mat Store, surnamed Zhu, said from the side that the boxes did not contain money, and if they did, the inspectors would be very happy. The inspectors, upon hearing this, harbored a grudge. They followed the coolies to the Yongfengrun Cloth Store and watched them open the boxes. When it was confirmed that they contained factory cloth, the inspectors withdrew. They returned to the entrance of the Kaitai Mat Store and brutally beat the clerk Zhu, causing injuries. Shop clerks from nearby stores, seeing this, rose up in indignation and dragged Zhu, Cai, and others to the National Salvation Association. As the Kaitai store clerk Zhu was a member of the Dongxi Pu fire brigade, the members of the brigade convened a meeting of fire brigades from various districts in the county chamber of commerce, proposing four conditions: (1) The anti-Japanese association's income and expenditure accounts should be made public; (2) The offending inspectors should be dismissed; (3) An apology should be made to the residents near Zidiling; (4) The offenders should be paraded through the streets as a warning. The above four items were submitted to the anti-Japanese association for a response. Wu Boyu, the standing chairman of the association, agreed to respond at a meeting on the afternoon of the 13th. Therefore, at around 2:00 PM yesterday, Chairman Wu convened a meeting of representatives from the fire brigade at the anti-Japanese association to discuss the matter. It was decided that the first item would be implemented after the accounts were cleared, the second item would be implemented, the third item would be waived, and for the fourth item, plainclothes police officers would escort the offending inspectors through the streets. The representatives considered this satisfactory. At 5:00 PM, Chief Inspector Lin of the Public Security Bureau led several plainclothes police officers, escorting Zhu Baoshun, Zhu Baoxun, and Cai Zhaogen, among others, from the meeting venue directly to Zidiling, then to North Street, past Caifengfang, and other places, parading them around for a week before returning.

Hefei Shenfu Bank Closes Down 107

Shenfu Bank, the most prominent and well-established bank in Dongda Street in this county, has been forced to close down due to being implicated by the closure of various other businesses, incurring debts of more than 200,000 yuan. Yesterday, it announced its closure. It is reported that it owes 110,000 yuan to the Shanghai Taiping Bank and is in the process of liquidation.

Poor Autumn Silkworm Harvest in Deqing 108

In recent years, the authorities have spared no effort in improving silkworm varieties. However, in rural areas, the adoption of improved varieties often does not yield as good results as local varieties, and most of them die midway. Deqing County has recently discovered this problem, which is attributed to the improper handling of the guiding director Huang Weimin and others. An appeal has been sent to the chairman of the Lake Society. The original telegram reads: "On August 6th, our county received 5,000 sheets of Tanguan brand autumn silkworm eggs from the Cuisheng seed production farm, issued by the Department of Construction, designated improved areas, distributed to the people, and assigned guiding director Huang Weimin and instructors to guide them in the villages. This demonstrates the great concern for the people's livelihood by the director of the Department of Construction of Zhejiang. The villagers, compelled by livelihood, competed to buy them, even resorting to pawning, borrowing, or even selling green seedlings and mulberry leaves for next spring. Unexpectedly, during the third or fourth instar stage, the silkworms did not molt uniformly, their sizes varied, and their bodies gradually withered. Upon checking the symptoms, it was found that the seeds contained a virus, which was due to the negligence of the guiding director Huang Weimin and the section chief of the construction section, Xu Sicong, who delayed the receipt of the seeds for three days and did not immediately unpack them and place them in a cool place, resulting in the silkworm eggs being heated. As a result, the autumn silkworms died completely. However, the villagers suffered great labor and financial losses. How should they be compensated? Your society is concerned about our hometown. Please do your best to find a solution and quickly telegraph the Department of Construction of Zhejiang to order the seed production farm to compensate for the losses and to severely punish the Yellow Director Weimin Xu and Section Chief Sicong who delayed the silkworm seeds to appease the people's debts. Respectfully awaiting orders. Representatives of silkworm farmers in the silkworm mulberry improvement area of Deqing County, Shen, sincerely bows."

Tibetan Troops Invade Yunnan, Urgent Police Report 111

Yunnan Association Receives Telegram from Yunnan Chairman

The Yunnan Association is organized by influential Yunnan and Kang provinces expatriates who are extremely concerned about the southwest border defense, cultural construction, and politics. The strength of the neighboring provinces necessitates caution. A slight misstep can bring about the pain of national subjugation. Tibetan guards have already yielded. Since the September 18th Incident, the Yunnan border and Xikang have repeatedly sounded alarms. The severity of the situation rivals that of the Northeast. The military in the provinces is engaged in internal strife. The central and southeastern regions are too distant to provide support, rendering them unable to plan border defense. As a result, the nation's territory shrinks by the mile, fostering unchecked growth. Recently, Zhongdian fell for several days and has yet to be recovered. Zhongdian connects the three provinces of Yunnan, Kang, and Tibet, and serves as Yunnan's main route into Tibet. It is an important military position that links with Atunzi and Lijiang, shielding western Yunnan. Unfortunately, due to being constrained by Liu of Sichuan, the local garrison was weak and overrun by thousands of Tibetans carrying the latest weapons. The entire territory fell, shaking Yunnan and Kang. Five or six days ago, the Shanghai Yunnan Association received this news and convened board members Xu Han, Song Chongjiu, Hu Zhongming, Feng Ruji, and others for discussion. It was decided to first telegraph Yunnan Chairman Long Yun and urge the provincial government to earnestly plan border defense and recover the territory by a set deadline. Yesterday morning, the association received an urgent telegram from Yunnan Chairman Long stating: "To the Yunnan Association, Jinshenfu Road, Shanghai, upon receiving the Blue Telegram, we have learned that thousands of unruly bandits have gathered in Zhongdian, and the county seat is indefensible, leading to its fall. We have received a telegram from Dalian Director Shi Hua stating that Independent Battalion Commander Li Congshan has led his troops to assist. The headquarters fears that the bandits are numerous and the troops are insufficient, so we have telegraphed Dalian to instruct Liu Brigade and Bu Corps to send the entire Third Battalion to assist in the suppression, and approve that Director Shi may, if necessary, deploy the Long Battalion stationed in Yongsheng to provide support. Also, the bandits are wearing military uniforms, suggesting a mastermind. We have telegraphed the General Staff Headquarters of the Central Government to request one or two fighter planes to be dispatched to the battlefield to investigate the bandits' rear situation to clarify the truth. Gentlemen, your distant inquiries demonstrate your concern for your hometown. This is a telegram in reply, expressing our gratitude. Long Yun bows, et cetera." It is reported that the association, considering the severity of the situation and its impact on national defense and the safety of Yunnan and Kang, will convene a board meeting on the 17th (Sunday) to discuss concrete measures.

The First Batch of American Cotton Will Arrive in Shanghai on Schedule 112

Arrival Expected on the 26th of This Month

Minister Song Conferred With Yarn Merchants

The first shipment of American cotton purchased under the Sino-American cotton and wheat loan agreement is confirmed to have arrived in Japan and is about to be shipped to Shanghai. Details of the key information are as follows:

American Cotton Arrives in Shanghai Via Japan 113

The first batch of 11,200 bales of cotton purchased by China under the American loan agreement left the port of New Orleans on the 15th of last month. The American company Fulae & Co. chartered the ship Asia Reliance to transport them via the Panama Canal to Shanghai. The company received a telegram from the shipowner yesterday stating that the ship is expected to arrive in Yokohama, Japan, today. However, the ship also contains goods for Japan and needs to stay in Japan to unload them. It will take approximately ten days, after which it will sail to Shanghai, arriving no later than the 26th of this month. This is the first shipment of American cotton to be brought to China under the loan agreement.

Warehouses Expedite Repairs and Modifications 114

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has reached an agreement with the Cotton and Wheat Transportation Management Office stationed in Shanghai by the Ministry of Finance. All of the American cotton, over 200,000 bales, will be stored in the company's warehouses after arriving in Shanghai. Liu Hongsheng has already spent more than 43,000 yuan to repair and modify the Yangzi Wharf. The first 11,200 bales of cotton will be unloaded in the warehouses at that wharf. Subsequent large shipments of American cotton will also be stored in that warehouse.

Exchanges of Views at Minister Song's Residence 115

After returning to Shanghai from Lushan, Minister Song recently conferred with Rong Zongjing, Guo Shun, Nie Lusheng, and others, leaders of Chinese cotton mills, at his residence on Qiqi Road regarding the purchase of American cotton by Chinese cotton mills and the rescue of Chinese cotton yarn. They merely exchanged views and did not make any specific decisions. Chinese cotton mills believe that this year's domestic cotton harvest is abundant, but the domestic yarn market remains sluggish, with accumulated yarn. Spinning yarn will inevitably result in losses. They hope to receive discounts on the price of American cotton and find ways to reduce the amount of stored yarn in order to reduce costs for the Chinese cotton mills.

National Goods Exhibition Opens Yesterday 116

Attended by Over 10,000 Representatives From All Walks of Life and Citizens

Wang Xiaolai Urged: "Don't Buy Things!"

The National Goods Movement Exhibition, organized by the First Special District Citizens' Federation of Shanghai and the China National Products Manufacturers' Federation, held its opening ceremony at Penglai Market in Xiaoximen at 2:00 PM yesterday. Over 10,000 representatives from all walks of life and citizens attended. Jiang Huaishu, representing the Municipal Party Headquarters, unveiled the exhibition. Mayor Wu's representative, Yu Hongjun, raised the flag. The ceremony was grand and reached a peak.

(Photo by Xu Tianzhang)

A Glimpse of the Venue 117

The exhibition venue is located between Penglai Road and Yongning Street in Ximen. Three pine and cypress arches were erected along the road, serving as the main entrances and exits. The venue is filled with temporary stores set up by various factories, displaying a wide variety of goods that are dazzling to the eye. Ladies from all walks of life were enthusiastically purchasing goods. In the center of the venue is a large ceremonial platform, with a portrait of Sun Yat-sen hanging in the middle and national flags on both sides. The center of the platform is reserved for the chairman and representatives from various sectors, with the record-keeping area on the right and the press area on the left. Two bottles of flowers are placed on the ceremonial table, creating a simple and orderly arrangement. Above the platform hangs the large banner of the China Products Improvement Society with the four characters "National Goods Save the Nation", which is particularly striking. The perimeter of the venue is maintained by police officers from the Public Security Bureau, as well as members of the Wu Yu, East Asia, and Boy Scouts.

Unveiling and Flag-Raising 118

At 2:30 PM, the Public Security Bureau military band played music to open the meeting. The members of the presidium, Wang Xiaolai, Wang Hanliang, Hu Fengxiang, Zhang Yilu, Chen Binghui, Liu Zhongying, Yu Zhongxian, and representatives from various party, government, and military circles entered the venue in an orderly fashion. Then, Jiang Huaishu, representing the Municipal Party Headquarters, unveiled the curtain in front of the platform, triggering thunderous applause from the audience. Next, under the leadership of the presidium, Mayor Wu's representative, Yu Hongjun, successively stepped down from the platform and walked to the tall flagpole planted in front of the gate. As the military music played a melodious tune, Yu held the long rope and hoisted the Blue Sky with a White Sun flag into the air, where it fluttered in the wind, which was quite magnificent. The citizens in the audience applauded and cheered. After the flag-raising ceremony, they returned to the presidium platform to hold the opening ceremony.

Chairman's Report 119

The presidium elected Wang Hanliang to give a report, which stated in brief: "Today, the First Special District Citizens' Federation of Shanghai and the China National Products Manufacturers' Federation are holding the National Goods Movement Exhibition here. We are honored to have so many guests participating. The purpose of holding this exhibition, of course, is to promote national goods. I hope that all compatriots will from now on buy national goods and not buy foreign goods, especially goods from enemy countries. You must know that most of the enemy's warships, planes, guns, and cannons are paid for with the money that flows out from our purchase of foreign goods. Therefore, the Chinese people must work together to preserve our money, purchase national goods, and expand our military equipment to increase our national strength, et cetera."

Speeches From All Walks of Life 120

Next, representatives from all walks of life gave speeches. (1) Jiang Huaishu from the Municipal Party Headquarters stated in brief: "The purpose of holding the National Goods Movement Exhibition is to promote national goods. When I heard the four words 'promote national goods,' I felt very heartbroken. May I ask how many national goods can be seen in the Shanghai market? Everywhere you look, you only see foreign goods. Whether it's for use or consumption, foreign goods are indispensable. The Chinese people's psychology of favoring foreign goods has reached such a point, how can the country not be weak and be bullied by others? Therefore, I propose that the products produced by every national goods factory should first be strictly inspected by the municipal chamber of commerce to determine whether the raw materials are national goods, and then be allowed to be sold on the market. Then, the citizens who love to use national goods will not mistakenly buy foreign goods, et cetera." (2) Yu Hongjun from the Municipal Government stated in brief: "At this time when the national crisis is serious and the people's livelihood is declining, everyone knows that promoting national goods is the only good policy to save the country. Because promoting national goods is the only way to open up a path for the Chinese nation and reverse the bankruptcy of rural areas. If the Chinese nation can revive and the rural economy does not go bankrupt, then all undertakings can be carried out boldly. This is the meaning of opening this National Goods Movement Exhibition today. At the same time, I also feel that there are two necessary conditions for promoting national goods: (1) The entire Chinese nation must thoroughly awaken; (2) All citizens must cooperate. Only in this way can we achieve the true goal of promoting national goods and not betray the meaning of today's meeting." (3) Ji Zejin from the Ministry of Industry said: "Opening this National Goods Exhibition today is of great significance. Since the beginning of trade with foreign countries, the entire market in the country has been filled with foreign goods. Whether it's everything we use in our daily lives, such as foreign cloth, foreign paper, foreign oil, foreign matches, foreign lamps, foreign porcelain, they are all foreign goods. It is even shameful that we, a country based on agriculture, are eating foreign rice and foreign wheat. The money of our country is being taken away by foreigners, how can our country not be poor? Therefore, to save the country, we must promote national goods. To promote national goods, we must first concentrate all national goods in one place, openly exhibit them, and jointly study and improve them to seek progress. This is the purpose of our National Goods Exhibition. This National Goods Exhibition is like setting up an introduction agency, specializing in introducing national goods to the Chinese people, so that the Chinese people can recognize national goods and non-national goods, and telling the Chinese people to use national goods and use less foreign goods. We hope that this exhibition will be held in major cities in the interior from Shanghai, and even in major cities in Europe and America to develop foreign trade. Then, this will be in line with the future of our country's industry, which is unlimited. Recently, Singapore will be preparing to hold an overseas national goods exhibition. If our country's goods factories can export national goods to the exhibition as much as possible, this is also an excellent opportunity to promote national goods overseas. I recently had a conversation with Mr. Kao, the Canadian Commercial Counselor, who said that the Canadian National Exhibition in Ottawa and the French National Exhibition in Paris are held once a year. We very much hope that our country will participate, but our country has never paid attention to it. In the future, I hope that national goods merchants will cooperate with the government and actively participate in these exhibitions at that time, so that although Chinese national goods cannot compete with them in foreign countries, they can gain an overseas market, which is not without benefit to the future of our country." Speakers who followed included Wu Huanru from the Social Affairs Bureau, Ye Jiaxing from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Ye Xianggao from the General Trade Union, and Mao Yong from the Second Special District Court (summaries omitted). Finally, Wang Xiaolai from the presidium gave a reply, stating in brief: "Today's opening of this National Goods Movement Exhibition is to promote national goods. However, the best way to promote national goods is not to buy (things). By 'things,' I mean goods from Eastern and Western countries. If we don't buy goods from Eastern and Western countries, then what (things) will dare to bully us? Therefore, I hope that the citizens will not go to buy (things) and buy national goods, et cetera."

Oath and Tour 121

After Wang finished his reply, everyone stood up straight, raised their right hands high, and unanimously swore to use national goods. The oath read: "We swear with sincerity to use national goods to fulfill our national duties. Having sworn, we will never change. We swear." After the oath, the presidium led leaders from various sectors on a tour of the factories' displays. After a light refreshment, they took photos and dispersed.

Today's program, from 2:00 PM to 9:00 PM, includes Shanghai martial arts, Wang Caiyun's Suzhou opera costume performance, Wang Xiaoxin's Shanghai opera, Mo Wuqi's magic, Zhu Guoliang's Suzhou opera costume performance, Yi Haoqi and Yi Haoxiao's comedy, and Lu Xiaowu's new drama. Shanghai Native Cloth Movement Conference Opens This Afternoon 124

Initiated by Nine Agencies Including the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau

Two-Week Exhibition to Improve Native Cloth

The Shanghai Native Cloth Movement Conference is scheduled to open at 1:00 PM this afternoon at the Municipal Public Education Center. The conference will last for two weeks, until the end of this month. Variety shows will also be added to enhance the fun. Details are as follows:

Organized and Initiated by the Social Affairs Bureau and Others 125

This conference is jointly organized by the Shanghai Municipal and County governments and initiated by nine agencies: the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, the Municipal Agricultural Association, the Municipal Public Education Center, the Tai Jiabao Native Cloth Improvement Association, the County Education Bureau, the County Farmers' Education Center, the Shanghai Native Cloth Store, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and the Chinese Cloth Clothing Association. A preparatory committee was organized beforehand, and Chen Songchun, Yu Zhenhui, and Zhang Ji were elected as standing members. Chen Dongbai will be the recorder, Wu Huanru will be the chief receptionist, and Shen Ruoxu will be the chief marshal.

Expanded Publicity, Entertainment, and Lectures 129

The conference's publicity matters are given special attention. It is in contact with various newspapers to publish special supplements and has requested the Municipal Education Bureau to order all cinemas to show advertisements promoting local cloth. In addition, lectures are scheduled to be held in the Minglun Hall at 1 PM every day on the 16th, 17th, 24th, and 30th, inviting Tai Shuangqiu, etc., to give lectures, as well as entertainment. Today's performers will be the People's Education Center's harmonica costumed speech, Shen Zhi San's Tan Huang, Li Zhaoxiong's magic, and the Lin Yin Elementary School kindergarten students' performance, etc.

Declaration of the Local Cloth Movement Conference 130

The declaration of the Shanghai Local Cloth Movement Conference states: "When it comes to saving the country today, those who talk are not as good as those who act, and those who aim far are not as good as those who plan for immediate success. Instead of seeking benefits for the people that are difficult to achieve, it is better to focus on their existing businesses and give them practical benefits, so as to save them in the present. We are initiating the Local Cloth Movement Conference amidst the severe national crisis and the collapse of the countryside. Some say that the momentum of the domestic goods movement is already on the rise, so why not plan and proceed in the direction of domestic goods, instead of dwelling only on local cloth? If not, set up factories and machinery for large-scale weaving plans to compete with imported cloth. If we don't consider this and only seek to expand handicrafts, isn't that out of touch with the times? There is nothing more wrong than this. They don't know that hand-woven local cloth is originally a handicraft unique to our Jiangsu Province. During leisure time from farming, weaving provides income to supplement the inadequacy of agricultural income. The sound of looms is heard in the neighborhood. Since the prevalence of foreign cloth, spinning and weaving have been cut off, and since the secondary industry has been cut off, the farmers' difficulties have become more serious. The reason for this is that there is no market for local cloth, and because the people of the country do not like to wear local cloth. We believe that the current domestic goods movement is being vigorously promoted, and local cloth is also a kind of domestic goods. We may as well take advantage of the situation to guide it, plan to improve it, and expand its sales. A great river does not abandon small streams, and mountains are based on plains. We hope that it will also be permitted by all enthusiastic patriots. As for the preparations, the matter is extremely simple. We will lend yarn and value to the original handicraft skills and original spinning and weaving equipment in the countryside to buy their finished products and promote their sales in the market. With a wave of the hand, the countryside already has a secondary industry to speak of, and the countryside already has hope for salvation. This is something that we can do, and it is not like a large-scale weaving factory that requires purchasing land, building houses, machinery and equipment, and raising assets. Our humble intention has always been to resist inferior goods and relieve the suffering of rural areas. We only hope that all patriotic gentlemen will rise up and advocate wearing it, then we will be fortunate."

Japanese Consul Demands to Transfer Jinshui Mountain, Public Security Bureau Refuses 131

Already Sent to the Garrison Headquarters for Interrogation

A Korean named Liu Yinfa, who became an American citizen and resided in the Lanxin Lane of Diswei Road, was suddenly shot in his residence a few days ago. The murderer was a young Korean. Subsequently, the Japanese Deputy Consul in Shanghai, Zuozhi Duozhu, and Goto Gentaro, a criminal from the Special High Police Section of the Police Department, together with the Fifth District Police Station, sent personnel to the Yisun ship in the Sixteenth Pier to arrest a suspect named Jinshui Mountain, who was temporarily detained in the Water Patrol Team. The Shanghai Public Security Bureau interrogated him in order to find out the truth. People in Shanghai, both Chinese and foreign, paid close attention to this case because it involved a political background.

Denies the Murder 132

According to Jinshui Mountain's statement to the Shanghai Public Security Bureau, he is 24 years old, his father's name is Jin Doutian, he is from Guangdong, and his mother, Huang, is Korean. He is currently serving as a special service chief in the Heavy Artillery Company of the Training Team of the Army Artillery School in Dingjiaqiao, Nanjing, with signature business cards and private seals as proof. During the January 28th Shanghai War, he came to Shanghai to participate in the battle and has a commemorative intention of the 19th Route Army's Shanghai War as proof. In June, the Nanjing team had a summer vacation, so he came to Shanghai and resided in the home of his friend Liu Xiong in Dongyouheng Road, which has been two months so far. This time, he took a ship back to Guangdong because of something, and was suddenly arrested on the ship. He doesn't know the reason for the arrest. When asked about the Liu Yinfa case, he claimed that he knew nothing about it and firmly denied the murder. The Shanghai Public Security Bureau then summoned Chen Lu, Liu Yinfa's housekeeper, to testify that the murderer was not this person at the time.

Refuse to Transfer 133

The Shanghai Public Security Bureau refused to transfer him on the grounds that Jinshui Mountain was a Chinese citizen and an active serviceman, and there was no evidence of the murder, so he was sent to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters for interrogation.

Beijing-Shanghai Train Derailed Twice Yesterday Morning 135

At around 10:00 AM yesterday morning, at the Hepingmen Station of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, Locomotive No. B-37, towing mud-carrying vehicles, drove out from the mud-transport branch line. Two of the rear wheels of the locomotive suddenly derailed and fell. The Nanjing Station dispatched craftsmen on a rescue train to repair it. At around 12:00 PM, the derailed locomotive was put back on track, and a test run was immediately conducted. Unexpectedly, the branch line, because it was made of old materials and had been in disrepair for many years, was showing signs of being unable to bear the load. Therefore, during the test run, the four front wheels of Locomotive No. 37 derailed again and fell between the main and branch lines, causing traffic to be blocked. Further repairs were carried out, and it was completed at around 3:00 PM. Therefore, the ninth express train from Beijing to Shanghai yesterday was delayed by more than two hours.

Shocking New Japanese Barracks 136

Open to the Public Yesterday

The Engineering is Truly Great

What are the Thoughts of the Chinese People?

Since the January 28th Incident, the Japanese Marine Corps Headquarters in Shanghai has become increasingly active. It demolished the old barracks and rebuilt a new, modern, and solid permanent large barracks on the original site at the end of North Sichuan Road, opposite Hongkou Park. Construction began in November of last year and was completed at the beginning of this month. A military hospital was also built next to the west side of the road and was completed at the same time. The Japanese Marine Corps authorities specially received Chinese and foreign newspaper reporters at 2:00 PM yesterday, allowing them to go to visit freely, and guided them to visit all levels on the surface for a week. The engineering is truly great, but a fleeting glance is not enough to see its mystery. Military secrets are even more out of the question. The details are as follows:

A Glimpse of the Bottom Layer 137

The reporters drove to the end of North Sichuan Road at 2:00 PM and got off in front of the Japanese Marine Corps Headquarters. The sentry with guns asked in Japanese whether they were newspaper reporters. A messenger soldier collected name cards one by one and invited them into a room to wait for a while. After the reporters entered the room, they first looked out the window to observe the outline of the building. The towering four-story building is styled somewhat like the Continental Shopping Mall on Nanjing Road and Jiujiang Road, but it is a three-sided encirclement. The middle is a square that can accommodate hundreds of soldiers for vertical and horizontal exercises. The bottom layer is generally equipped with armored vehicles, tanks, light artillery vehicles, machine guns, machine feet vehicles, military transport vehicles, military vehicles, etc. At that time, a large number of transport vehicles were carrying countless rectangular wooden boxes. The appearance was like the new barracks of the Japanese Marine Corps (photographed by Li Zunyong).

Like coffins in the army, hundreds of soldiers unloaded them one by one from the cars and moved them upstairs. According to Japanese reporters, after the soldiers' bedding is bundled, every three sets are placed in a wooden box, which is used as tables and chairs during the day, which is also very convenient for transportation. These hundreds of soldiers had just arrived in Shanghai from Japan and were about to be transferred to Hankou.

Visit Layer by Layer 138

While observing, the messenger soldier invited Mr. Kashiwagi Setsu, a translator in casual Western clothing, to bow and greet them and invite them upstairs. The escalators can accommodate five or six people walking side by side. The cement steps are unusually flat, and the copper handrails are unusually flat. The internal form is a surrounding corridor, which is also quite wide. The west side is all inner rooms. The offices and rooms of important personnel such as the commander and the staff are all on the first floor. The second and third floors are gradually dormitories for middle and lower-level officers and soldiers. The windows on all sides along the road are very small. Judging from its walls, it is strangely thick, and the power of shells is not capable of igniting it. Under the leadership of the translator, reporters and others took a quick look and had no time to observe in detail. There are several doors that are shaped like gates and are equipped with huge locks. I don't know what is hidden inside. There are no signs outside the door, and there is no way to see its mystery.

Rooftop View 139

Finally, to the rooftop, wide can accommodate Thousands of people, junior soldiers, sit Under the sun, operating chores very diligently. Since the January 28th Incident, reporters have inspected the inside of Japanese soldiers many times, and they all have this impression. There are no idle pastimes like those of our country's soldiers after a full meal. The watchtower is built here, with the flag of the rising sun flying in the wind. One day, a soldier at the top of the platform carried out his watch work. Its height is said to be one hundred feet from the ground. Next to the watchtower is a shrine for soldiers to worship. Two or three of our compatriots are still building it. The style is small, and it is made into a rockery shape, and then a wooden merchant is built on top of it. Next to the shrine is a monument commemorating the January 28th Incident, with an inscription on the monument that says, (Shanghai Marine Corps Recruitment Society), followed by (Written by Marshal Earl Togo Heihachiro on July 7th), written by Japanese Marshal Togo to commemorate the Marine Corps soldiers annihilated by the 19th Route Army on January 28th.

No Secrets 140

After the visit of each layer has been completed, a An exit from the floor, placed high The shooting machine gun is like the place where he first climbed to the roof, because he realized that the flat and solid roof is not only able to shoot machine guns, but also install several heavy artillery guns to freely destroy this great Shanghai. After going downstairs, resting in the reception room on the bottom floor, a glass of soda and a few cigarettes, the translator answered questions from guests at will. The former staff officer, Kakuda, although he did not know anything except Japanese, also represented Commander Sugiyama to socialize with Chinese and foreign reporters and guests, shaking hands and saluting very busy. According to him and translator Kashiwagi Setsu, there is no such thing as a ground-level building, and there are no secrets.

Densely Packed Wires 141

There is a radio on the roof that receives sound. Pole, ground wires crisscross densely It is also arranged, and it has not been fully installed There are also. Above the atrium, the power lines are as dense as spiderwebs. On the left side of the lower floor, there is a room for the general receiving and dispatching office of the telegraph, which is also being equipped with various machines. There is also a Japanese sign posted outside the door strictly prohibiting entry, which shows the strictness of its communication network. The soldiers' lives are completely scientific. When entering the cafeteria, they must disinfect and wash their hands. The training of sports is even stricter, with special sports rooms and wrestling rooms. The discipline is strict and sufficient for our people to learn.

Attached Hospital 142

After the reporters quit, Fu Cheng Kakuda Staff's good intentions, guide Across Huanglu Road to the same completion of the Naval Hospital for inspection, the building is also four stories, but the location is very narrow, covering only a few acres, compared with the large barracks, there are large and small witches. From the lowest floor are the office, pharmacy, diagnosis and surgery rooms, floor by floor, set up venereal disease, ophthalmology, dentistry, infectious disease, and other treatment rooms, and dozens of large and small sick rooms. Although the house is newly built, the large and small wards are already crowded with beds. The reporters saw that the notices written on the walls and the nurses' reports were consistent with the phenomenon of overcrowded wards. The rumor in Japanese newspapers that many of the Shanghai Marine Corps suffered from dysentery is not false.

Construction Process 143

Japanese barracks houses grow in a square shape, covering an area of about More than fifty acres, up to four stories high, The whole house can accommodate five or six thousand people, there is a wide square in the middle, which can be used for training. At the top floor of the intersection of North Sichuan Road and Doulean Road, there is a watchtower, about sixty feet high, which can be used to command the entire army to fight. The construction of the camp began in November last year, and it took only six months to complete. The drawings of the barracks were drawn by the Japanese Ministry of the Navy, and special commissioners and technicians were sent to Shanghai to supervise the construction. All materials were transported to Shanghai by transport ships specially sent by the Ministry of the Navy, without freight charges or taxes. However, the price has reached more than 1.5 million Japanese gold. The hospital's house is also four stories high, fully equipped, and the cost is huge. When the reporter returned and wrote this, he felt a myriad of emotions, and his hands trembled and his heart broke.

China Merchants Bureau Ship Supervisors Resist Handover, Bureau Compels Implementation 144

China Merchants Bureau General Manager Liu Hongsheng's dismissal of ship supervisors has provoked opposition from the Seamen's Union and resistance from the supervisors, which has been delayed for months. Now that the Ministry of Communications has issued an order, it will be forcibly implemented yesterday. A dispute may come to an end. The details are recorded as follows:

Supervisors Resist 145

The ship supervisors to be replaced include Jianghua, Jiangyu, Jiangxin, Jiangda, and Xinjiangtian, a total of six ships. Huongsheng, according to the public presentation of the crew members of each ship and the investigation by the personnel, should apply to the board of directors for approval and issue a bureau order in late July for implementation. Among them, the two ships, Xinjiangtian and Jianghua, resisted the most fiercely. At first, the preparatory committee of the Seamen's Union came forward to oppose it, and then resisted the handover, causing the successors to be unable to take over. In the past two months, the supervisors have even feigned illness and have not gone to the ship, and have sent their wives to the ship to take over their duties in order to resist the implementation of the transfer in a passive way. The bureau believed that women on board were not in good shape, so it took compulsory measures.

Ministry Order Arrives in Shanghai 146

After the preparatory committee of the Seamen's Union opposed the matter, Liu Hongsheng turned to the Ministry of Communications to state the reasons for adjusting the crew and transferring the supervisors in order to reorganize the shipping affairs. On the 14th, the Ministry of Communications issued a reply, which has arrived at the bureau, saying that the bureau's adjustment of personnel in order to rectify shipping affairs is a duty that should be handled, how can others come out to obstruct it, which hinders the bureau's administration. The general manager's transfer of ship supervisors is approved. However, the preparatory committee of the Seamen's Union must be properly replied to. This is of the utmost importance. After the Ministry's order arrived at the bureau, General Manager Liu immediately complied with it and ordered the supervisors who resisted to hand over their duties.

Compulsory Execution 147

Among the ships, Jianghua supervisor Zhang Jinxian resisted the most strongly. Recently, because the bureau limited the handover of duties and the handover of public property in the ship, Zhang faked illness and did not arrive, and sent his wife to the ship to work. The bureau could not bear it any longer, so it ordered the shipping department to notify Jiangyu supervisor Fan Xinbiao to prepare to take over Jianghua's supervisor duties. However, because Zhang Jinsheng avoided meeting and refused to hand over, the bureau notified the Water Public Security Team on the 14th and sent many police officers to the Jianghua ship at the South Bund Pier. Under the surveillance of the water police, the public property of the supervisor's department was taken out for inspection and handed over to the new supervisor Fan Xinbiao for safekeeping to carry out his mission. If there is any missing public property, Zhang will still have to be recovered from Zhang, and Zhang Jinsheng, who resisted the order, was reassigned to Jiangyu as a supervisor, and he was forced to hand over.

Reply to the Union 148

The supervisor of Xinjiangtian also resisted the handover and is now being handled by Liu Hongsheng together. Xinjiangtian now needs to be suspended and sent to the factory for major repairs, with Xin Ming acting as a substitute. During the suspension period, the supervisor is ordered to hand over, otherwise, the police will be sent to forcibly hand over in accordance with the Jianghua precedent. On one side, the bureau replied to the Seamen's Union, stating that the dispute, which had been delayed for more than a month, has been resolved in accordance with the order of the ministry.

It was measured once in 1926, and it will be re-measured this year. The results obtained can also prove whether the theory of continental drift is true. It is said that the French will stay in Shanghai for three months and will be staying at the Xujiahui Observatory.

New Regulations for Tax on Tobacco and Alcohol 153

Tax Administration Issues Announcement Yesterday

Order Seven Provinces and Regions to Comply

The Taxation Administration of the Ministry of Finance issued an announcement yesterday on the taxation of tobacco and alcohol throughout the country in accordance with the new regulations, saying, "For the purpose of announcement, after investigation, the opening of public sales of tobacco and alcohol has been going on for many years, but the results have not been obvious, and long-standing malpractices have become increasingly serious. The reason for this is that although the tax system may not be perfect, the collusion between merchants and contractors is the biggest reason. Once the collecting agency contracts out the tax amount, it only holds those who are subcontracted accountable for the amount, and no longer asks about how it is collected. After the merchants contract, they only know how to allocate the amount and use it for private purposes. The tax rates and regulations are just a formality. As a result, superiors and subordinates deceive each other and肆其侵蝕The loopholes in it are inextricable. Since this Administration was ordered to concurrently operate the tobacco and alcohol tax, it has been observing the situation in various provinces for a year and deeply knows where the crux lies. If the system of layers of contracting is not abolished, it is not enough to talk about rectification. This time, the native tobacco leaves are subject to special tax, and the native wine is changed to a fixed-amount tax, which focuses on clearing up long-standing malpractices and verifying and auditing. Within the seven provinces and regions of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Henan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and Fujian, all native tobacco leaves that have paid the special tax must be filled in with a tax payment certificate. As for the affixing of stamps on packages, native wines that have paid the fixed-amount tax, in addition to the tax payment certificates for retail sales that should be cut and retained, the part of the container must be affixed with a tax payment certificate. In this way, the foundation of innovation is established, and the evil practices of contractors must be prohibited. In short, after the implementation of the new regulations, the collecting agencies should abide by the regulations and earnestly implement them, and must not follow the old story of recruiting merchants and contracting. Merchants must also not collude with collecting personnel to allocate taxes to merchants. If both parties continue to do things as usual and there are still things, once discovered or accused, they will be severely punished and will not be lenient. I am afraid that many other merchants are not aware of it, so I hereby clarify the original intention of the reform and earnestly inform everyone so that everyone knows it. The various凛遵 shall not violate this announcement."
